11/13/24, 5:47â€¯PM - Akshay Sir: https://www.linkedin.com/posts/taniya-khatri-47a21416b_hiring-uiuxinternship-internshipopportunity-activity-7262421698535137280-8vE0?utm_source=share&utm_medium=member_android
11/13/24, 6:27â€¯PM - Akshay Sir: These are some of the Mini Projects which you can build inorder to learn Nodejs.
Those who already know NodeJS can proceed with more complex Projects.


URL Shortener:
Create a URL shortening service that takes a long URL as input and generates a shortened version.

When a user visits the shortened URL, they should be redirected to the original long URL.

You can use Express and a database like MongoDB to store the mappings between the short and long URLs.

Expense Tracker: Develop an expense tracking application where users can input their expenses, categorize them, and generate reports or visualizations of their spending habits.

You can use packages like Chart.js or Plotly.js to create charts and graphs.

File Uploader:
Create a file uploader using Node.js and a package like multer.

Users should be able to select and upload files, which should be stored on the server.

You can add features like file validation, resizing, and handling different file types.

Currency Converter:
Create a currency converter application that fetches real-time exchange rates from an API and allows users to convert between different currencies.

You can use packages like axios to make API requests and display the converted results.

To do App:
Build a command-line to-do list application using Node.js.

Users should be able to add, delete, and mark tasks as completed.

You can use libraries like readline or inquirer to interact with the user through the command line.

Web Scraper:
Create a web scraping tool that extracts specific information from web pages.

Users should be able to provide a URL and specify the elements or data they want to scrape.

You can use packages like Cheerio or Puppeteer for web scraping.

Authentication System:
Implement user authentication and registration using Node.js and a package like Passport.js.

Users should be able to sign up, log in, and log out.

You can use a database like MongoDB to store user information securely.


Chat Application:
Build a real-time chat application using Node.js and Socket.IO.

Users should be able to join chat rooms, send messages, and receive messages in real-time.

Socket.IO makes it easy to implement real-time communication between the server and clients.

1/11/25, 3:41â€¯PM - Ankur Sir: Dear Students,

We are delighted to announce that this semester, your GATE CSE classes will be conducted by our esteemed faculty members:

Akshay Sir (M.Tech, IIIT Hyderabad)
Rahul Sir (M.Tech, IIT Bombay)
Suraj Sir (M.Tech, IIIT Bangalore)
With their exceptional expertise in cracking competitive exams like GATE, PGEE, and ISRO Scientist recruitment, they will guide you through the following GATE CSE subjects:

Programming (C Language) & Data Structures
Algorithms
Operating Systems
DBMS
Computer Networks
Computer Organization & Architecture (COA)
Discrete Mathematics
Theory of Computation
Compiler Design
Digital Logic
Engineering Mathematics
General Aptitude
Class Schedule and Features:

Classes will be held on Monday, Wednesday, and Friday, with 2-hour sessions each day.
Each session will cover in-depth concept explanations followed by hands-on problem-solving exercises.
You will be provided with a comprehensive set of questions to ensure exam readiness.
Regular tests will be conducted to assess your preparation level.
Dedicated doubt-clearing sessions will be arranged to help you overcome any challenges.
We highly encourage you to make the most of this incredible opportunity provided by the institute. These classes are designed to strengthen your grasp of technical subjects, which will not only prepare you for GATE but also significantly boost your placement readiness. Many top companies, emphasize on technical subjects like Programming, Data Structures, Algorithms, Operating Systems, DBMS, Computer Networks, COA, and related GATE CSE topics during their hiring processes including technology giants like
 Google,Microsoft,Amazon, Semiconductor and Hardware Companies like
Qualcomm, Intel,AMD,
Nvidia,Texas Instruments, 
Product-Based Tech Companies
Adobe,Oracle, Cisco and Startups and Unicorns like Flipkart, Ola, 
Consulting and Service-Based Companies like TCS Digital,
Infosys Specialist Roles,Wipro Turbo,Deloitte, Research and Development Roles like
ISRO, DRDO,BARC, 
,Adobe Research.
These companies often test candidates on foundational technical subjects through coding challenges, system design problems, and technical interviews, making it crucial to have a strong command of these areas.

Additionally, the knowledge gained will be invaluable for excelling in other competitive exams such as CAT, Bank PO, SSC CGL, RBI Grade B, UPSC, and various state-level public service commission exams. The strong analytical, logical reasoning, and problem-solving skills developed through these subjects will also give you an edge in assessments for roles in government organizations like DRDO, ISRO, BARC, and Indian Railways. Moreover, this foundation is equally beneficial for private sector exams conducted by firms like TCS (NQT), Infosys, and Cognizant.

6/30/25, 4:42â€¯PM - Devesh Sir: Dear All,
 
HSBC has launched India Business Case Program 2025-26: Empowering Youth for Career Readiness.
 
Eligibility Criteria:
Eligible Course: All UG Course (2026 & 2027 passing out batch only)
No Percentage Criteria
 
About the Program:
This program offers a unique learning opportunity for youth to enhance their employability and leadership skills and provides students from across India an opportunity to demonstrate their ability and skills at the annual HSBC-University of Hong Kong (HKU) Asia-Pacific Business Case program.
 
About India Business Case program:
The India Business Case program is supported by HSBC India and is implemented by United Way of Mumbai and Sattva Consulting. The program features hybrid training workshops, interactions with industry professionals and masterclasses, providing participants with practical insights and real-world business perspectives. It progresses through 5 rounds, starting with a preliminary round at the college level, followed by a video pitch round and two regional rounds, finally culminating in a national round in Mumbai. The top two teams stand a chance to represent India at the HSBC-University of Hong Kong (HKU) Asia-Pacific Business Case program â€“ a premier program that brings together teams of undergraduate students from countries in the Asia-Pacific region.

The 2021 Asia-Pacific round was even won by an Indian team, which was selected through the India Business Case program.

In 2024-25, the program received nearly ~8,000 student registrations from 158 colleges across the country. Students in the national round also got the opportunity to engage with top business leaders.
This year, we are delighted to invite students from your esteemed institution to register for the program. We believe this is an incredible opportunity for your students to apply their theoretical learnings in a practical context.

The India Business Case program aims to offer exposure through:
In-person regional workshops, focused on building knowledge and skills useful in solving business case studies, which are often part of campus-hiring processes of companies as well as consulting firms
Video pitch rounds for the students to assess their problem solving and presentation skills
Opportunity for national round finalists to interact with industry professionals and gain valuable insights on leadership. 
 
Students can register online by filling this registration form. Kindly circulate the same to ensure maximum participation in the program. For more details regarding the program, please refer to the FAQ sheet attached to this email and the recap video from last year here.

Reward for the Winning Team:
The top 2 teams at the National Finals will receive support to travel to Hong Kong, for participating in the HSBC/University of Hong Kong Asia Pacific Business Case Competition 2026. The winning team in Hong Kong has the opportunity to receive prize money of $ 10,000.

Please find enclosed a detailed FAQ sheet for the program. All interested participants/ institutions can reach out to ibcp.registrations@sattva.co.in in case of any queries.
